event = {
	id = 131180
	random = no
	country = USA

	name = "EVT_131180_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131180_DESC"
	picture = "american_surrender"
	persistent = yes
	style = 0

	trigger = {
		war = { country = SOV country = USA }
		control = { province = 606 data = SOV } #DC
		OR = {
			lost_VP = { country = USA value = 70 }
			lost_IC = { country = USA value = 70 }
			lost_national = { country = USA value = 70 }
			AND = {
				nuked = { data = -1 where = 606 }	#DC
				OR = {
					lost_VP = { country = USA value = 65 }
					lost_IC = { country = USA value = 65 }
					lost_national = { country = USA value = 65 }
				}
			}	
		}
		NOT = {
			event = 131299
			event = 131240
			event = 131230

		}

	}

event = {
	id = 131220
	random = no
	country = JAP

	trigger = {
		war = { country = JAP country = USA }
		control = { province = 663 data = JAP } # Pearl Harbor
		NOT = {
			control = { province = 1786 data = USA } #Wake
			control = { province = 1624 data = USA } #Guam
			control = { province = 658 data = USA } #Hawaii
		}
		OR = {
			OR= {
				# West Coast
				control = { province = 761 data = JAP } #San Diego
				control = { province = 762 data = JAP } #Los Angeles
				control = { province = 765 data = JAP } #San Francisco
				control = { province = 764 data = JAP } #Sacramento
				control = { province = 783 data = JAP } #Portland
				control = { province = 780 data = JAP } #Seattle
			}
			NOT = {
				battleship = { country = USA value = 6 }
				carrier = { country = USA value = 6 }
			}

event = {
	id = 131240
	random = no
	country = USA

	name = "EVT_131240_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_131240_DESC"
	picture = "american_surrender"
	persistent = yes
	style = 0

	trigger = {
		war = { country = JAP country = USA }
		control = { province = 606 data = JAP } #DC
		OR = {
			lost_VP = { country = USA value = 70 }
			lost_IC = { country = USA value = 70 }
			lost_national = { country = USA value = 70 }
			AND = {
				nuked = { country = USA data = -1 where = 606 }	#DC
				OR = {
					lost_VP = { country = USA value = 65 }
					lost_IC = { country = USA value = 65 }
					lost_national = { country = USA value = 65 }
				}
			}	
		}
		NOT = {
			event = 131299
			event = 131230
			event = 131180
			event = 131250
			event = 131270
		}
		random = 50
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 14
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 75
		name = "EVT_131240_ACTA"
		command = { type = leave_alliance }
		command = { type = independence which = CAN value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = independence which = MEX value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = independence which = MAN value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = independence which = U87 value = 1 when = 0 }	#DHSA0.4
		command = { type = independence which = MEN value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = independence which = SIA value = 1 when = 0 }
		command = { type = independence which = PHI value = 1 when = 0 }	#遠藤マイクロ
		command = { type = end_mastery which = PHI }
		command = { type = end_mastery which = LIB }
		command = { type = end_mastery which = CAN }

	style = 0

		war = { country = GER country = USA }
		NOT = { 
			control = { province = 606 data = USA } #DC
			control = { province = 606 data = GER } #DC
			control = { province = 606 data = JAP } #DC
		}
		OR = {
			lost_VP = { country = USA value = 70 }
			lost_IC = { country = USA value = 70 }
			lost_national = { country = USA value = 70 }

				nuked = { country = USA data = -1 where = 606 }	#DC

					lost_VP = { country = USA value = 65 }
